My old Ford Ranger was having trouble switching in the low gears and was making horrible noises. So I decided to take it in to AA Gears Shafts very highly recommended by my neighbours across the street.
The initial surprise I had was the employees' attention and the time they spent explaining what they thought might be wrong. Highly professional and very kind service.
This is my go to place.</text>

< Text>
I'm surprised I haven't given this store a review, yet. Lol

Anyway, I've been shopping here for awhile now, and, for the comic book nerd, this store is GREAT!! As mentioned by other commenters, as well as the store itself, they have a HUGE supply of Funko Pops, ones that you won't or can't find in Hot Topic, Game Stop, or F.Y.E. (which are all in the mall). What I like is the proprietor carries a lot of hard-to-find action figures, as well as the occasional statue or figurine. He has a neat assortment of things, which make for great browsing, if nothing else.< /Text>

It is shocking and unacceptable!!!!!! I told them I consider myself high risk because my sister had died at the age of 66 and she had waited too long for her initial mammogram and was at stage 2 by the time she had it done. Nothing.

< text>
I have never left a review for anything, but I feel very strongly about my experience this time. For the past 5 years, or perhaps longer, I have been going to this facility for my mammograms and ultrasounds, and my experience has always been nothing short of wonderful, UNTIL now. Although the front staff was mildly polite, the interaction to follow was indiscreet, impersonal, and unprofessional. The back of the facility was unkempt with dirty laundry piled high in their hampers, broken lockers, and cheap offerings of tea and coffee with missing condiments. I remember when the staff was very warm, personal but highly professional, and spoke with each client quietly and discreetly. They never loudly discussed the details of insurance nor demanded payment upfront...NEVER. The back of the facility was always clean and put together and their lockers were very well-maintained. They always had a fully stocked beverage area as well. Their attention to detail was impeccable. I certainly appreciated the warmth, professionalism, and discretion they offered their patients during such an invasive and vulnerable time. Unfortunately, this time around, this facility has FAILED to deliver any of the services that made me come back year-after-year. The atmosphere of the facility seemed altogether unwelcoming, even with respect to the technicians. Normally, my appointments would take longer and felt very thorough. This time, it felt fast and rushed. Although I do not know what the technician is required to do, I think my experience leading up to my appointment already colored my perspective. Unfortunately, I will no longer be going to this facility again. I can only hope that there is another one out there that can provide the same level of service that this facility USED TO offer.< /text>
